\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{aws\_timestamp\_convert()}{aws\_timestamp\_convert()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint64\+\_\+t aws\+\_\+timestamp\+\_\+convert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint64\+\_\+t}]{timestamp,  }\item[{enum \mbox{\hyperlink{clock_8h_a1c88a4b2ee9a32347fd7901c0fe948d9}{aws\+\_\+timestamp\+\_\+unit}}}]{convert\+\_\+from,  }\item[{enum \mbox{\hyperlink{clock_8h_a1c88a4b2ee9a32347fd7901c0fe948d9}{aws\+\_\+timestamp\+\_\+unit}}}]{convert\+\_\+to,  }\item[{uint64\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{remainder }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Copyright Amazon.\+com, Inc. or its affiliates. All Rights Reserved. SPDX-\/\+License-\/\+Identifier\+: Apache-\/2.\+0. Converts \textquotesingle{}timestamp\textquotesingle{} from unit \textquotesingle{}convert\+\_\+from\textquotesingle{} to unit \textquotesingle{}convert\+\_\+to\textquotesingle{}, if the units are the same then \textquotesingle{}timestamp\textquotesingle{} is returned. If \textquotesingle{}remainder\textquotesingle{} is NOT NULL, it will be set to the remainder if convert\+\_\+from is a more precise unit than convert\+\_\+to. To avoid unnecessary branching, \textquotesingle{}remainder\textquotesingle{} is not zero initialized in this function, be sure to set it to 0 first if you care about that kind of thing. If conversion would lead to integer overflow, the timestamp returned will be the highest possible time that is representable, i.\+e. UINT64\+\_\+\+MAX. \mbox{\Hypertarget{preamble_8h_ac7acb5bce882e2f6b07d4e084facdd7d}\label{preamble_8h_ac7acb5bce882e2f6b07d4e084facdd7d}}
